  * grade_story_101.txt (grade=6.2)
    The characters of Edrin and Liora show promise but lack depth. Edrin's welcoming nature is established, but his motivation beyond collecting artifacts remains vague. Liora's "weathered heart" is told rather than shown through specific experiences. Their interactions feel somewhat formulaic, with dialogue that explains themes directly rather than revealing character through nuanced exchanges. The characters serve the story's message more than existing as fully realized individuals.
